- 000020 *********************************************************************
- 000020 If you want your HTML5 build to play in-browser from itch.io:
- 000020  - Edit your itch.io project page as follows, if you haven't already:
- 000020     'Kind of project': HTML
- 000020  - Find the 'html5' file, and make sure its
- 000020     "This file will be played in the browser" checkbox is checked.
- 000020  - Then check the 'Embed options' section
- 000020  - Don't forget to click 'Save'!
- 000020 Note: 'HTML' project pages on itch still offer the non-web downloads!
- 000020 
- 000020 If you _don't_ want it to play in-browser from itch.io:
- 000020  - Edit your itch.io project page as follows, if you haven't already:
- 000020     'Kind of project': Downloadable
- 000020  - Find the 'html5' file, and click its
- 000020     "Hide this file and prevent it from being downloaded" checkbox.
- 000020  - Don't forget to click 'Save'!
- 000020 *********************************************************************
